	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" >Sergio Ramos</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		<div id="contentSub2"></div>
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Spanish professional footballer</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about the Spanish association football player. For the Portuguese basketball player, see <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A9rgio_Ramos" title="Sérgio Ramos">Sérgio Ramos</a>. For the Mexican water polo player, see <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ramos_(water_polo)" title="Sergio Ramos (water polo)">Sergio Ramos (water polo)</a>.</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">In this <a href="/wiki/Spanish_name" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish name">Spanish name</a>, the first or paternal&#32;<a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">surname</a> is <i> Ramos</i>&#32;and the second or maternal family name is <i> García</i>.</div>

<p><b>Sergio Ramos García</b> (<small>Spanish pronunciation:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">[sexjo ramoz ai.a]</a></span>;<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;A&#93;</a></sup> born 30 March 1986) is a Spanish professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Centre-back" class="mw-redirect" title="Centre-back">centre-back</a> and <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captains</a> both <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spanish national team</a>. He has also played as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">right-back</a> earlier in his career.<sup id="cite_ref-realrb_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-realrb-4">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Hailed as one of the greatest defenders in the history of the sport, he has received praise for his leadership and goalscoring capabilities.<sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_defenders_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_defenders-6">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After emerging through <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a>'s youth academy and spending two seasons with the senior side, Ramos moved to Real Madrid in the summer of 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-realrb_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-realrb-4">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Since then, he has gone on to become a mainstay for Real Madrid, and has won 22 major honours, including five La Liga titles and four <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> titles, becoming one of La Liga's top goalscorers from a defensive position. He played a crucial part in the build-up to all four UEFA Champions League wins, being named in the competition Squad of the Season each time. He also notably scored the equaliser in the 93rd minute of the <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2014 UEFA Champions League Final">2014 UEFA Champions League Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ramos has been named to the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="FIFPro">FIFPro World11</a> eleven times; a record for a defender, and the third-most all-time. He has also been elected to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> nine times, also a record for a defender and the third-most of any player. Additionally, Ramos has been named <a href="/wiki/La_Liga_Awards" title="La Liga Awards">La Liga's Best Defender</a> a record five times, and to the <a href="/wiki/La_Liga_Awards" title="La Liga Awards">La Liga Team of the Season</a> in <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_La_Liga" title="2015–16 La Liga">2015–16</a>.
</p><p>Internationally, Ramos represented the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spanish national team</a> at four <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">World Cups</a> and three <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship" title="UEFA European Championship">European Championships</a>. He won the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship" title="UEFA European Championship">UEFA European Championship</a> in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">2008</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">2012</a>, being named to the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#All-Star_Team" title="FIFA World Cup awards">FIFA World Cup Dream Team</a> in 2010, and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship_Teams_of_the_Tournament" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA European Championship Teams of the Tournament">UEFA Euro Team of the Tournament</a> in 2012. He made his first appearance for Spain at the age of 18 and, in 2013, he became the nation's youngest player to ever reach <a href="/wiki/List_of_men%27s_footballers_with_100_or_more_international_caps" title="List of men&#39;s footballers with 100 or more international caps">100 caps</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Young_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Young-8">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Ramos currently holds the record as the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team#Most_capped_players" title="Spain national football team">most capped player</a> in the history of the Spanish national team, and is his country's eighth-highest <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team#Top_goalscorers" title="Spain national football team">all-time goalscorer</a>. He also holds the record of most international victories for Spain with 130 matches.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sevilla">Sevilla</span></h3>
<p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Camas,_Seville" title="Camas, Seville">Camas, Seville</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andalusia" title="Andalusia">Andalusia</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Ramos started playing at Camas C.F. by the age of 6,<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> then he began his career at local side <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a>, emerging through the club's youth system alongside <a href="/wiki/Jes%C3%BAs_Navas" title="Jesús Navas">Jesús Navas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Puerta" title="Antonio Puerta">Antonio Puerta</a>. He made his first-team – and <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> – debut on 1 February 2004, coming on as a 64th-minute <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">substitute</a> for <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Gallardo" class="mw-redirect" title="Francisco Gallardo">Francisco Gallardo</a> in a 0–1 away loss against <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_de_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo de La Coruña">Deportivo de La Coruña</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_La_Liga" title="2004–05 La Liga">2004–05 season</a>, Ramos appeared in 41 games as Sevilla finished sixth and <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_UEFA_Cup" title="2005–06 UEFA Cup">qualified</a> to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Cup</a>, scoring in home fixtures against <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a> (2–1)<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> (2–2).<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_UEFA_Cup" title="2004–05 UEFA Cup">the season's edition</a> of that European tournament, he scored his first continental goal, heading to conclude a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/CD_Nacional" class="mw-redirect" title="CD Nacional">CD Nacional</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Ramon_S%C3%A1nchez_Pizju%C3%A1n" class="mw-redirect" title="Estadio Ramon Sánchez Pizjuán">Estadio Ramon Sánchez Pizjuán</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_UEFA_Cup_first_round" title="2004–05 UEFA Cup first round">first round</a> (4–1 aggregate).<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Madrid">Real Madrid</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2005.E2.80.9309:_Record_transfer_and_early_days"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2005–09:_Record_transfer_and_early_days">2005–09: Record transfer and early days</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:192px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ramos_10mar2007.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Sergio_Ramos_10mar2007.jpg/190px-Sergio_Ramos_10mar2007.jpg" decoding="async" width="190" height="253" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Sergio_Ramos_10mar2007.jpg/285px-Sergio_Ramos_10mar2007.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Sergio_Ramos_10mar2007.jpg/380px-Sergio_Ramos_10mar2007.jpg 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="959" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ramos_10mar2007.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ramos in action in March 2007</div></div></div>
<p>In the summer of 2005, Ramos was purchased by Real Madrid for €27&#160;million, a record for a Spanish defender.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He was the only Spanish player brought in during <a href="/wiki/Florentino_P%C3%A9rez" title="Florentino Pérez">Florentino Pérez</a>'s first stint as Real's president.
</p><p>At the club, Ramos was assigned the number 4 shirt, previously worn by <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Hierro" title="Fernando Hierro">Fernando Hierro</a>. On 6 December 2005 he netted his first goal for the <i>Merengues</i>, in a 1–2 <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2005–06 UEFA Champions League">group stage loss</a> at <a href="/wiki/Olympiacos_F.C." title="Olympiacos F.C.">Olympiacos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During his first seasons, Ramos played as centre back, being also used as an emergency <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfielder</a> on occasion. However, with the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Christoph_Metzelder" title="Christoph Metzelder">Christoph Metzelder</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pepe_(footballer,_born_1983)" title="Pepe (footballer, born 1983)">Pepe</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_La_Liga" title="2007–08 La Liga">2007–08 season</a>, he was again relocated to right back. In his first four seasons at Real Madrid, Ramos displayed a goalscoring instinct unusual to many defenders, netting more than 20 goals overall. He also received the first nine of his 24 red cards for the club, including four in <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2005–06 Real Madrid CF season">his debut season</a>. His first red card came after two bookable offences in a 1–0 away loss to <a href="/wiki/RCD_Espanyol" title="RCD Espanyol">RCD Espanyol</a> on 18 September 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-retrospective_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-retrospective-18">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_La_Liga" title="2006–07 La Liga">2006–07 season</a>, Ramos scored five goals, including one in a 3–3 draw with <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">FC Barcelona</a>, as Real Madrid won a record 30th <a href="/wiki/List_of_Spanish_football_champions" title="List of Spanish football champions">Spanish league championship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 May 2008, he assisted <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_Higua%C3%ADn" title="Gonzalo Higuaín">Gonzalo Higuaín</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Last-minute_goal" title="Last-minute goal">89th minute</a> against <a href="/wiki/CA_Osasuna" title="CA Osasuna">CA Osasuna</a> in an eventual 2–1 away win, the match that sealed the club's 31st league championship. On the final day of the season, he scored twice in a 5–2 home win against already relegated <a href="/wiki/Levante_UD" title="Levante UD">Levante UD</a>: one through a header, and another an individual effort; these goals taking his league tally for the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_La_Liga" title="2007–08 La Liga">2007–08 season</a> to five.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 24 August 2008, Ramos scored in the <a href="/wiki/2008_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2008 Supercopa de España">2008 Supercopa de España</a> second leg against <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a>, making the score 2–1 in an eventual 4–2 and 6–5 aggregate win. The victory came despite Real Madrid playing with only nine men for a long period of time after <a href="/wiki/Rafael_van_der_Vaart" title="Rafael van der Vaart">Rafael van der Vaart</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ruud_van_Nistelrooy" title="Ruud van Nistelrooy">Ruud van Nistelrooy</a> were sent off. Although Ramos experienced a slight dip in form during the early part of the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2008–09 Real Madrid CF season">2008–09 season</a>, he returned to his best and on 11 January 2009, scoring an acrobatic volley in a 3–0 triumph at <a href="/wiki/RCD_Mallorca" title="RCD Mallorca">RCD Mallorca</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> He continued his scoring run the following week in a 3–1 home win against Osasuna.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ramos was named in both <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a>'s 2008 <i>Team of the Year</i>, adding the FIFPro Team of the Year 2007–08 accolade. He also finished 21st in the European Player of the Year nomination for 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2009.E2.80.9315:_Breakout_and_team_mainstay"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2009–15:_Breakout_and_team_mainstay">2009–15: Breakout and team mainstay</span></h4>
<h5><span id="2009.E2.80.9310_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2009–10_season">2009–10 season</span></h5>
<p>At the start of the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_La_Liga" title="2009–10 La Liga">2009–10 season</a>, Ramos was appointed as one of Real Madrid's four captains. Because Pepe had suffered a serious knee injury during this campaign, Ramos was often deployed as central defender. He scored four goals in 33 league matches; and, on 21 February 2010 he played his 200th official match for the <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">capital</a> team against <a href="/wiki/Villarreal_CF" title="Villarreal CF">Villarreal CF</a> (150 in the first division). Despite these personal highlights, <i>Los Blancos</i> finished the campaign without picking up any silverware.
</p>
<h5><span id="2010.E2.80.9311_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010–11_season">2010–11 season</span></h5>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:192px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Control_de_Sergio_Ramos.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/Control_de_Sergio_Ramos.jpg/190px-Control_de_Sergio_Ramos.jpg" decoding="async" width="190" height="217" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/Control_de_Sergio_Ramos.jpg/285px-Control_de_Sergio_Ramos.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/Control_de_Sergio_Ramos.jpg/380px-Control_de_Sergio_Ramos.jpg 2x" data-file-width="877" data-file-height="1000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Control_de_Sergio_Ramos.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ramos in action in October 2010.</div></div></div>
<p>In Real Madrid's 0–5 loss at Barcelona on 29 November 2010, Ramos was <a href="/wiki/Ejection_(sports)" title="Ejection (sports)">sent off</a> after kicking <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> from behind, then pushing <a href="/wiki/Carles_Puyol" title="Carles Puyol">Carles Puyol</a> in the ensuing melée.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> After this ejection, he equalled <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Hierro" title="Fernando Hierro">Fernando Hierro</a>'s previous record of ten red cards at the club, despite having played in 264 fewer games.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On 20 April 2011, Ramos started in <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Copa_del_Rey" title="2010–11 Copa del Rey">the season</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_del_Rey_Final" title="2011 Copa del Rey Final">final</a>, a 1–0 win against Barcelona in <a href="/wiki/Valencia" title="Valencia">Valencia</a>. In the subsequent victory procession, while celebrating on the top of the club's bus, he accidentally lost hold of the cup, which fell under the wheels of the vehicle; the trophy was dented as a result.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="2011.E2.80.9312_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2011–12_season">2011–12 season</span></h5>
<p>On 12 July 2011, Ramos extended his contract with Real Madrid until 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> The following 25 April, in the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_UEFA_Champions_League#Semi-finals" title="2011–12 UEFA Champions League">Champions League semi-finals' second leg</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">FC Bayern Munich</a>, he missed his <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalty shootout</a> attempt as Real Madrid lost 1–3;<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> the league campaign ended in conquest after a four-year wait, and he was the player with most balls recovered in his team, third overall.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="2012.E2.80.9313_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2012–13_season">2012–13 season</span></h5>
<p>On 9 January 2013, Ramos was sent off for a second <a href="/wiki/Penalty_card#Yellow_card" title="Penalty card">bookable offense</a> midway through the second half of an eventual 4–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Celta_de_Vigo" class="mw-redirect" title="Celta de Vigo">Celta de Vigo</a> for <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Copa_del_Rey" title="2012–13 Copa del Rey">the domestic cup</a>. He subsequently received a four-match suspension, after it was revealed he also insulted <a href="/wiki/Referee_(association_football)" title="Referee (association football)">referee</a> Miguel Ángel Ayza Gámez.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> The following month, mere minutes after scoring the second goal at home against <a href="/wiki/Rayo_Vallecano" title="Rayo Vallecano">Rayo Vallecano</a> and less than 20 minutes into the first half, he received two yellow cards within one minute in the eventual 2–0 home success, taking his red card tally with Real Madrid alone to 16; and 12 in the league.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In late February/early March 2013, due to the absence of <a href="/wiki/Iker_Casillas" title="Iker Casillas">Iker Casillas</a> due to injury, Ramos <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captained</a> Real to back-to-back wins over Barcelona in just four days: he netted the 2–1 home winner in the second game, heading home after a <a href="/wiki/Corner_kick" title="Corner kick">corner kick</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2013–14_season">2013–14 season</span></h5>
<p>On 14 December 2013, Ramos received a <a href="/wiki/List_of_Real_Madrid_CF_records_and_statistics" title="List of Real Madrid CF records and statistics">club record</a> 18th red card for Real Madrid in a 2–2 draw at Osasuna,<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> but the suspension was later lifted.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> His 19th came in a 3–4 home defeat to Barcelona, on 23 March 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-retrospective_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-retrospective-18">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 26 April, Ramos scored a header against Osasuna in <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> at the Bernabéu, in a counter-attack which he began with a strong tackle. It was his first goal in La Liga in six months, since his volley against Levante on match-day 8.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> On 29 April 2014, Ramos scored two headers in four minutes in a 4–0 away win against Bayern Munich in <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League">the semi-finals of the Champions League</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> with the tie ending with a 5–0 aggregate score and Madrid's <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2014 UEFA Champions League Final">qualification to the decisive match</a> for the first time in twelve years. Ramos' brace against Bayern (4 minutes) was the fastest brace in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> semi-final history at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> On 4 May, Ramos scored in the 2–2 draw with Valencia at home in <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> with another header, scoring in back-to-back league games.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Just three days later, Ramos scored his first free-kick for a 1–1 draw away to Valladolid, having scored in three consecutive La Liga matches and scoring four consecutive matches for Real Madrid for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> On 24 May, in the final against <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>, he headed home in stoppage time to tie the game 1–1, and Real Madrid went on to win 4–1 in <a href="/wiki/Overtime_(sports)" title="Overtime (sports)">extra time</a> to claim 'La Decima', their tenth trophy in the competition; he was also chosen by fans as <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the match">Man of the match</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Ramos ended <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2013–14 Real Madrid CF season">2013–14</a> with 7 goals, which made it his highest scoring season for Real Madrid at the time.
</p>
<h5><span id="2014.E2.80.9315_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–15_season">2014–15 season</span></h5>
<p>Ramos started <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2014–15 Real Madrid CF season">2014–15 season</a> on 12 August 2014 by playing the full 90 minutes in a 2–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> to win their first trophy of the season, the <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2014 UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a>. He then played the two-legged <a href="/wiki/2014_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2014 Supercopa de España">Supercopa de España</a> final against <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> with <i>Los Blancos</i> losing 2–1 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Ramos scored his first goal of the season on 31 August in week two of <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_La_Liga" title="2014–15 La Liga">La Liga</a>, a header in a 4–2 away loss against <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Ramos scored his 50th Real Madrid goal which came off his knee on 8 November against Rayo Vallecano at the Bernabéu in La Liga as Real Madrid won 5–1.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He scored in both the semi-final and <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2014 FIFA Club World Cup Final">the final</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA Club World Cup">2014 FIFA Club World Cup</a> and was voted the Player of the Match in both as Real Madrid won the tournament in Morocco. Ramos was also voted the player of the tournament, winning the Golden Ball.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.93present:_Captaincy_and_sustained_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–present:_Captaincy_and_sustained_success">2015–present: Captaincy and sustained success</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ramos_desde_el_balc%C3%B3n_de_la_Presidencia_de_la_Comunidad_de_Madrid_con_la_%C3%9Andecima_Copa_de_Europa.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Sergio_Ramos_desde_el_balc%C3%B3n_de_la_Presidencia_de_la_Comunidad_de_Madrid_con_la_%C3%9Andecima_Copa_de_Europa.jpg/180px-Sergio_Ramos_desde_el_balc%C3%B3n_de_la_Presidencia_de_la_Comunidad_de_Madrid_con_la_%C3%9Andecima_Copa_de_Europa.jpg" decoding="async" width="180" height="277" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Sergio_Ramos_desde_el_balc%C3%B3n_de_la_Presidencia_de_la_Comunidad_de_Madrid_con_la_%C3%9Andecima_Copa_de_Europa.jpg/270px-Sergio_Ramos_desde_el_balc%C3%B3n_de_la_Presidencia_de_la_Comunidad_de_Madrid_con_la_%C3%9Andecima_Copa_de_Europa.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Sergio_Ramos_desde_el_balc%C3%B3n_de_la_Presidencia_de_la_Comunidad_de_Madrid_con_la_%C3%9Andecima_Copa_de_Europa.jpg/360px-Sergio_Ramos_desde_el_balc%C3%B3n_de_la_Presidencia_de_la_Comunidad_de_Madrid_con_la_%C3%9Andecima_Copa_de_Europa.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1433" data-file-height="2205" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ramos_desde_el_balc%C3%B3n_de_la_Presidencia_de_la_Comunidad_de_Madrid_con_la_%C3%9Andecima_Copa_de_Europa.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ramos posing with the European Cup, after the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">2015–16 season</a></div></div></div>
<h5><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season">2015–16 season</span></h5>
<p>Ramos agreed a new five-year contract with Real Madrid in August 2015, tying him to the club until 2020. He was also made captain after the transfer of Casillas to <a href="/wiki/FC_Porto" title="FC Porto">FC Porto</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> On 8 November, Ramos scored his first goal of the season away to Sevilla, it was an overhead kick which forced him to get substituted due to landing on his injured left shoulder.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 20 December 2015, Ramos captained Madrid to a 10–2 victory over <a href="/wiki/Rayo_Vallecano" title="Rayo Vallecano">Rayo Vallecano</a>, the club's highest scoring La Liga victory in 55 years.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> The following 13 March, he received his 20th red card for Real Madrid in a 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/UD_Las_Palmas" title="UD Las Palmas">Las Palmas</a>, having earlier scored the game's opening goal with a header from an <a href="/wiki/Isco" title="Isco">Isco</a> corner kick. On 2 April 2016, he returned from suspension in a 2–1 victory against Barcelona at <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a>, where he was again sent off, receiving his 21st red card and fourth in a <a href="/wiki/El_Cl%C3%A1sico" title="El Clásico">Clásico</a> fixture.<sup id="cite_ref-retrospective_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-retrospective-18">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Real Madrid reached the <a href="/wiki/2016_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2016 UEFA Champions League Final">2016 UEFA Champions League Final</a>, where they faced <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>. Ramos once again scored in a final, putting Real ahead in the first half. At the time, he was just the fifth player to score in two different Champions League Finals after Raul, <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Eto%27o" title="Samuel Eto&#39;o">Samuel Eto'o</a>, Lionel Messi and Cristiano Ronaldo. After a second-half equaliser from Atlético, he then scored a penalty in the shoot-out which resulted in Madrid winning 5–3; thus, he lifted his first UEFA Champions trophy as a captain.<sup id="cite_ref-2015–16_CL_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2015–16_CL-50">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> According to author <a href="/wiki/Michael_Cox_(journalist)" title="Michael Cox (journalist)">Michael Cox</a>, he also notably "tipped the balance of the game toward Real Madrid" by tripping <a href="/wiki/Yannick_Carrasco" title="Yannick Carrasco">Yannick Carrasco</a> up and stopping a three-on-one counter in stoppage time, with 30 seconds remaining and the score 1–1.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> He was named <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the match">man of the match</a> by <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> after the game.<sup id="cite_ref-2015–16_CL_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2015–16_CL-50">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> By winning the final, Real Madrid earned the right to play against the winners of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Europa League">2015–16 UEFA Europa League</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/2016_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2016 UEFA Super Cup">2016 UEFA Super Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Ramos ended <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2015–16 Real Madrid CF season">2015–16</a> with three goals in 33 games which was his lowest goal tally and the fewest matches he played in any season at Real Madrid due to ongoing injuries.
</p>
<h5><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17_season">2016–17 season</span></h5>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Felicidades_al_Real_Madrid,_campe%C3%B3n_de_liga_(34824732435).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/Felicidades_al_Real_Madrid%2C_campe%C3%B3n_de_liga_%2834824732435%29.jpg/230px-Felicidades_al_Real_Madrid%2C_campe%C3%B3n_de_liga_%2834824732435%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="230" height="138" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/Felicidades_al_Real_Madrid%2C_campe%C3%B3n_de_liga_%2834824732435%29.jpg/345px-Felicidades_al_Real_Madrid%2C_campe%C3%B3n_de_liga_%2834824732435%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/Felicidades_al_Real_Madrid%2C_campe%C3%B3n_de_liga_%2834824732435%29.jpg/460px-Felicidades_al_Real_Madrid%2C_campe%C3%B3n_de_liga_%2834824732435%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5555" data-file-height="3334" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Felicidades_al_Real_Madrid,_campe%C3%B3n_de_liga_(34824732435).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ramos and Community of Madrid President <a href="/wiki/Cristina_Cifuentes" title="Cristina Cifuentes">Cristina Cifuentes</a> with the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_La_Liga" title="2016–17 La Liga">2016–17 La Liga</a> trophy during celebrations in Madrid.</div></div></div>
<p>Ramos started in the Super Cup, scoring Real Madrid's second goal of the match in the 93rd minute, and hence bringing the game into extra-time. Real Madrid were the eventual 3–2 winners, with Ramos being named <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the match">man of the match</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 3 December 2016, he scored his fourth Clásico goal, an equaliser against Barcelona in a 1–1 draw at the <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a> in the 90th minute, extending Madrid's unbeaten run to 33 games.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> One week later, he scored another late goal, this time after 92 minutes, to help Madrid claim a 3–2 victory against <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_de_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo de La Coruña">Deportivo de La Coruña</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> On 15 January 2017, Ramos scored an own goal late in the game against Sevilla which equalised the score at 1–1 and eventually Real Madrid lost the match 2–1 in stoppage time, thus ending their unbeaten streak at 40 matches.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> A week later, he scored both goals in a 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A1laga_CF" title="Málaga CF">Málaga</a>, registering his 50th goal in La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 February, in a 3–1 victory against <a href="/wiki/CA_Osasuna" title="CA Osasuna">Osasuna</a>, Ramos's marked his 500th match with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> Round of 16-second leg, Ramos scored an important equalising header against <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">S.S.C. Napoli</a> in a 3–1 away win as Real Madrid qualified to the quarter-final after winning 6–2 on aggregate. On 12 March, Ramos scored another late header winner for Real Madrid, this time against <a href="/wiki/Real_Betis" title="Real Betis">Real Betis</a> at the Bernabéu in a 2–1 win, taking his goal tally to 10 for the season – scoring double digit goals in a season for the first time in his career. Ramos' winner put Real Madrid back at the top of the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_La_Liga" title="2016–17 La Liga">La Liga</a> table.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Real Madrid won their 33rd <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_La_Liga" title="2016–17 La Liga">La Liga</a> title, giving Ramos his fourth league title overall and first as captain.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> They went on to win their first league and European Cup double since 1957–58 season, as the team defeated <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2017 UEFA Champions League Final">2017 UEFA Champions League Final</a>. This also made Ramos the first man to captain a team to back-to-back European Cups in the <a href="/wiki/European_Cup_and_UEFA_Champions_League_history#1993_–_The_birth_of_the_Champions_League_and_Marseille_attain_first_title" class="mw-redirect" title="European Cup and UEFA Champions League history">Champions League era</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> His ten goals in <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2016–17 Real Madrid CF season">2016–17</a> made it the highest scoring season of his career.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span></h5>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:249px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Real_Madrid_C.F._the_Winner_Of_The_Champions_League_in_2018_(1).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Real_Madrid_C.F._the_Winner_Of_The_Champions_League_in_2018_%281%29.jpg/247px-Real_Madrid_C.F._the_Winner_Of_The_Champions_League_in_2018_%281%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="247" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Real_Madrid_C.F._the_Winner_Of_The_Champions_League_in_2018_%281%29.jpg/371px-Real_Madrid_C.F._the_Winner_Of_The_Champions_League_in_2018_%281%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Real_Madrid_C.F._the_Winner_Of_The_Champions_League_in_2018_%281%29.jpg/494px-Real_Madrid_C.F._the_Winner_Of_The_Champions_League_in_2018_%281%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Real_Madrid_C.F._the_Winner_Of_The_Champions_League_in_2018_(1).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ramos hoisting the <a href="/wiki/European_Champion_Clubs%27_Cup" title="European Champion Clubs&#39; Cup">European Champion Clubs' Cup</a> as Real Madrid celebrate winning the UEFA Champions League, on <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Champions League Final">26 May 2018</a></div></div></div>
<p>On 20 August 2017, in Real Madrid's first game of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_La_Liga" title="2017–18 La Liga">2017–18 La Liga</a>, he received his 23rd career red card. It was his 18th in La Liga, a joint highest record. He went on to break that record, seeing his 19th La Liga red in a 0–0 draw with <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Ramos scored his first goal of the season on 13 September in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, scoring a bicycle kick against <a href="/wiki/APOEL_FC" title="APOEL FC">APOEL</a> on match-day 1.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_La_Liga" title="2017–18 La Liga">La Liga</a>, Ramos scored four goals, including two penalties – against Leganes and Sevilla. During the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">2017–18 UEFA Champions League</a>, he made eleven appearances, while scoring one goal, when Madrid won their third consecutive and 13th overall Champions League title.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Ramos' performance in <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Champions League Final">the final</a>, however, was met with criticism;<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> a challenge on <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Salah" title="Mohamed Salah">Mohamed Salah</a> resulted in the Egyptian dislocating his shoulder and missing the rest of the game,<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> and he hit Liverpool keeper <a href="/wiki/Loris_Karius" title="Loris Karius">Loris Karius</a> in the head with his elbow, the goalkeeper later being diagnosed with concussion.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Ramos later denied that he intentionally hit Karius, saying that <a href="/wiki/Virgil_van_Dijk" title="Virgil van Dijk">Virgil van Dijk</a> pushed him into Karius.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Ramos became the first player to captain a team to three consecutive Champions League triumphs, having now lifted the Champions League in every season as captain.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span></h5>
<p>Ramos began the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2018–19 Real Madrid CF season">2018–19</a> season scoring a penalty in the eventual 2–4 loss to Atletico Madrid in the <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2018 UEFA Super Cup">2018 UEFA Super Cup</a>. Taking the penalty ensured Ramos would be the team's new penalty taker with the departure of <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> On 26 August 2018, Ramos scored another penalty in Real Madrid's 1–4 away win against <a href="/wiki/Girona_FC" title="Girona FC">Girona FC</a>, making him the only player along with <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> to score in each of the last 15 <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> One week later, Ramos scored his third penalty of the season, against Leganes in a 4–1 win at the Bernabéu – his first goal at the Bernabéu since March 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 20 October 2018, Ramos played his 400th La Liga match for Real Madrid in a 1–2 loss at home to Levante, becoming only the tenth Real Madrid player to reach this milestone.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> After a run of poor results and the sacking of <a href="/wiki/Julen_Lopetegui" title="Julen Lopetegui">Julen Lopetegui</a>, Ramos scored his first goal for Real Madrid in two months through a <a href="/wiki/Panenka_(penalty_kick)" title="Panenka (penalty kick)">Panenka</a>, against Real Valladolid in <a href="/wiki/Santiago_Solari" title="Santiago Solari">Santiago Solari</a>'s first <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_La_Liga" title="2018–19 La Liga">2018–19 La Liga</a> game in charge of Los Blancos.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Two weeks later, on 11 November, Ramos scored another Panenka against <a href="/wiki/Celta_Vigo" class="mw-redirect" title="Celta Vigo">Celta Vigo</a> – making them the 25th different team he scored against in La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> This was Ramos' third Panenka from his last four penalties, with the inventor of the penalty, <a href="/wiki/Anton%C3%ADn_Panenka" title="Antonín Panenka">Antonín Panenka</a>, saying Ramos was the best 'imitator' of his penalty technique.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> With five goals in the first three months of the season, Ramos had his best goal-scoring start to a season at Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA Club World Cup">2018 FIFA Club World Cup</a>, Ramos played in both Real Madrid's semi-final against Kashima Antlers and the Final against Al Ain. Ramos scored a header in <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA Club World Cup Final">the final</a> as Real Madrid won 3–1 to claim their third consecutive FIFA Club World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> Ramos became the first player to lift three consecutive <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="FIFA Club World Cup">FIFA Club World Cups</a> while also becoming the first defender to score in two Club World Cup Finals.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 January 2019, Ramos scored a penalty in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Copa_del_Rey" title="2018–19 Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> game against <a href="/wiki/CD_Legan%C3%A9s" title="CD Leganés">Leganés</a>, which was his 100th career goal, excluding 2 goals for Sevilla's <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_Atl%C3%A9tico" title="Sevilla Atlético">reserve team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> To celebrate the goal, Ramos chose to show the number 100 with his fingers.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> On 24 January, Ramos scored a brace (2 goals) against <a href="/wiki/Girona_FC" title="Girona FC">Girona</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Copa_del_Rey" title="2018–19 Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey quarter-final first leg</a> in a 4–2 home win.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> It was Ramos' 4th brace for Real Madrid and his first in the Copa del Rey.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Ramos scored his 10th goal of the campaign with a header against <a href="/wiki/RCD_Espanyol" title="RCD Espanyol">Espanyol</a> in a 2–4 away win, which was also his 60th <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> goal.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> With ten goals to his name, Ramos equaled his highest-scoring season at Real Madrid which he set in <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2016–17 Real Madrid CF season">2016–17</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 February 2019, Sergio Ramos was playing in <a href="/wiki/El_Cl%C3%A1sico" title="El Clásico">the Clásico</a> for the 40th time. The captain has played in more encounters between Real Madrid and Barcelona than any other member of the current squads.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Three days later, in the <a href="/wiki/Madrid_Derby" title="Madrid Derby">Madrid Derby</a>, Ramos scored his eighth penalty of the season and his 11th goal in all competitions – making it his best goal-scoring season at Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, in the Champions League Round of 16 first leg away win over Ajax, Ramos became just the seventh player to play 600 matches for Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> In the match against Ajax, Ramos was booked for what seemed to be a needless challenge in the 90th minute. The booking meant that Ramos would miss the second leg against Ajax at the Bernabéu due a suspension of accumulating yellow cards. This sparked controversy after Ramos hinted to journalists in a post match interview that the yellow card was deliberate, which violates <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a>'s rules.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> Two and a half weeks later, UEFA opened a disciplinary investigation regarding this matter and decided to give Ramos a two-game ban, meaning he will also miss both the Champions League Round of 16-second leg against Ajax and the quarter-final first leg were Real Madrid to qualify.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> Due to Real Madrid's elimination, the suspension carried onto the next season and Ramos missed the first Champions League game of the 2019–20 season against <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 17 February, Ramos played his 601st match for Real Madrid, against Girona in La Liga, equaling the record of Real Madrid legends <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Hierro" title="Fernando Hierro">Hierro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Gento" title="Francisco Gento">Gento</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Ten days later, Ramos played in his 41st El Clásico, in the Copa del Rey semi-final second leg at home. This was Ramos' 602nd match for Real Madrid, taking up to him fifth in Real Madrid's all-time appearances list.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> On 2 March, Ramos played in the La Liga El Clásico at the Bernabéu, making him equal the all-time record of Sanchís, <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Gento" title="Francisco Gento">Gento</a> and <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a> by playing in 42 Clasicos.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> On 5 March, Real Madrid were eliminated from the Champions League by Ajax after losing 4–1 at the Bernabéu (aggregate 5–3).<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Ramos did not feature due to being suspended after forcing a yellow card in the first leg, thus faced criticism for doing so.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> Moreover, Ramos faced even more criticism as he was caught with a camera crew in the stands, filming for his new <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Prime" title="Amazon Prime">Amazon Prime</a> documentary.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> Ramos took to his <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Instagram" title="Instagram">Instagram</a> accounts to discuss the controversy surrounding his actions in which he admitted forcing the yellow card against Ajax in the first leg 'was an error and I take the blame 200%'. Regarding filming the documentary, Ramos claimed there were 'certain commitments' made prior and he did not imagine the game would pan out as it did.<sup id="cite_ref-marca.com_100-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-marca.com-100">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> Ramos picked up a calf injury at the start of April which saw him miss the rest of the campaign and the final eight La Liga matches.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span></h5>
<p>Ramos' first goal of the season was a header in his first <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2019–20 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> match of the campaign, against <a href="/wiki/Club_Brugge_KV" title="Club Brugge KV">Club Brugge</a> on 1 October at the Bernabéu. The goal came at a vital time as Real Madrid were 0–2 down by half-time but were able to make a comeback after another header by <a href="/wiki/Casemiro" title="Casemiro">Casemiro</a>. This was also Ramos' first Champions League goal in two seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> On 30 October, Ramos scored from the penalty-spot in a 5–0 home victory over <a href="/wiki/CD_Legan%C3%A9s" title="CD Leganés">Leganés</a>, continuing his run of scoring in 16 straight La Liga seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> One week later, on 6 November, Ramos scored his first penalty in the Champions League, which came against <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K." title="Galatasaray S.K.">Galatasaray</a> in a 6–0 home win. It was another 'Panenka' style penalty and also meant that Ramos scored in two Champions League group matches in the same season for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> On 18 December, Ramos played in his 43rd El Clasico, claiming the all-time appearance record for this historic fixture.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 January, Ramos scored the winning penalty in a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">shoot-out</a> against Atletico Madrid in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a_Final" class="mw-redirect" title="2019–20 Supercopa de España Final">Supercopa de España Final</a> in <a href="/wiki/Jeddah" title="Jeddah">Jeddah</a> as Real Madrid won 4–1 on penalties after a 0–0 draw after <a href="/wiki/Overtime_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Overtime (association football)">extra time</a>. This was the first time in Ramos' career that he scored a winning penalty in a shoot-out.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> The 2020 Super Copa title was Ramos' 21st trophy with Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> A month later, Ramos scored another header in La Liga, this time away to <a href="/wiki/CA_Osasuna" title="CA Osasuna">Osasuna</a> as Real Madrid won 4–1 to maintain top position in the table.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> Ramos' goal at El Sadar meant that he had scored in 20 different La Liga stadiums.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> This was Ramos' first La Liga goal of 2020, meaning he was the only player to score in La Liga in each of the last 17 calendar years – dating back to 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 26 February 2020, Ramos equalled the record of red cards received in the UEFA Champions League. With four red cards, he shares the unwanted record with <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Edgar_Davids" title="Edgar Davids">Edgar Davids</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-goal.com_111-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal.com-111">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> This dismissal came in a 2–1 home defeat to <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> in the Round of 16 first leg, for a <a href="/wiki/Professional_foul" title="Professional foul">Professional foul</a> on City striker <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Jesus" title="Gabriel Jesus">Gabriel Jesus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-goal.com_111-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal.com-111">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, Ramos featured in Real Madrid's 2–0 win over Barcelona at the Bernabéu in La Liga to leapfrog them into first place.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> This was Ramos' 21st consecutive Clasico in all competitions and his 30th in La Liga with Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When La Liga restarted after a three-month hiatus due to the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Spain" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Spain">COVID-19 pandemic</a>, Ramos scored in Real Madrid's first game back against <a href="/wiki/SD_Eibar" title="SD Eibar">Eibar</a> on 14 June at the <a href="/wiki/Alfredo_di_St%C3%A9fano_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Alfredo di Stéfano Stadium">Alfredo di Stéfano Stadium</a> in a 3–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> He also scored the first goal at this stadium in its inaugural match in May 2006.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> Ramos' goal began with him winning the ball back from Eibar's attack a few meters outside Madrid's own penalty area and ran 70 meters across the pitch to find the pass from <a href="/wiki/Eden_Hazard" title="Eden Hazard">Eden Hazard</a> to score his first La Liga goal from open play in over five years.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> On 21 June, Ramos scored a penalty for Real Madrid in their 1–2 win against Sociedad at the <a href="/wiki/Anoeta_Stadium" title="Anoeta Stadium">Anoeta</a>, which was the 20th consecutive penalty he converted for club and country (including shoot-outs).<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Ramos scored a free-kick against in a 2–0 win over Mallorca at the Alfredo di Stefano to become La Liga's All-Time scoring defender with 68 goals, surpassing <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Koeman" title="Ronald Koeman">Ronald Koeman</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> Ramos' free-kick was also his eighth La Liga goal of the season, making it his most prolific league campaign to date and his tenth in all competitions – hitting double figures for a third season.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> On 28 June, Ramos featured in the 0–1 away league win against Espanyol, heading the ball down right outside the Espanyol penalty area to <a href="/wiki/Karim_Benzema" title="Karim Benzema">Benzema</a> who eventually assisted Casemiro to score the winner right before half-time.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> This was Ramos' 645th match for Madrid, moving him up to fourth in the club's All-Time appearances list joint with <a href="/wiki/Santillana_(footballer)" title="Santillana (footballer)">Santillana</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> On 2 July, Ramos scored his fifteenth consecutive penalty for Real Madrid in the 79th minute which proved to be the winner in a narrow 1–0 home win against Getafe – opening up a four-point advantage at the top of La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> This was Ramos' ninth league goal of the season – equaling the record set by <a href="/wiki/Ezequiel_Garay" title="Ezequiel Garay">Ezequiel Garay</a> in 2006–07 for a defender with the most goals in a single La Liga season.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> The penalty against Getafe meant that Ramos had equaled his best goal scoring season (11 goals) which was set last season. Ramos had now scored in four out of six of Madrid's matches since the restart, more than any other player.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> Moreover, the goal was his 100th career club goal, and his 70th in La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> The win over Getafe was Ramos' 450th La Liga as a Real Madrid player, becoming just the fifth player to reach this milestone.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he scored another penalty – his 22nd in a row, and his tenth goal of the season in La Liga – in a 1–0 away win over Athletic Bilbao.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> He also became the first centre-back to score 10 goals in a La Liga season since <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Hierro" title="Fernando Hierro">Fernando Hierro</a> during the 1993–94 season.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> On 19 July, Ramos scored his eleventh league goal in Real Madrid's last La Liga game of the season against Leganes in an eventual 2–2 draw, making it his most prolific season in White with 13 goals across all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the season, Ramos won his fifth league title with Los Blancos.<sup id="cite_ref-Liga_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liga-132">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span></h5>
<p>On 27 September 2020, Ramos opened his goal count for the season after netting the winning goal against Betis from the penalty spot at <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Benito_Villamar%C3%ADn" title="Estadio Benito Villamarín">Estadio Benito Villamarín</a> in a 3–2 league win.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> One month later on 24 October in El Clasico, Ramos earned and converted a penalty at the Camp Nou in a 3–1 league win – this was his 25th consecutive penalty goal for both club and country (including shoot-outs).<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> Ramos' fifth El Clasico goal equaled the record of Ronald Koeman (who was in the other dugout) as the defenders with the most goals in this historic fixture. This was also Ramos' 31st consecutive La Liga Clasico, meaning he hasn't missed one since joining Los Blancos in 2005 – equaling Raul and Gento as the players who played in the most league Clasicos.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Ramos made his <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> debut for the season against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a>, assisting Casemiro's 93rd minute equaliser in a 2–2 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> This was Ramos' 16th Champions League campaign with Real Madrid, equaling the record of club legend and former teammate Iker Casillas.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> On 31 October, Ramos became just the 10th player to play 500 La Liga matches (461 for Real Madrid and 39 for Sevilla), as Madrid beat <a href="/wiki/SD_Huesca" title="SD Huesca">Huesca</a> 4–1 at the Di Stefano Stadium.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> On 3 November, Ramos scored his 100th goal for Real Madrid in all competitions, in a 3–2 win over <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> in the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_international_career_and_2006_FIFA_World_Cup">Early international career and 2006 FIFA World Cup</span></h3>
<p>In 2004, Ramos became an instant hit for <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_under-19_football_team" title="Spain national under-19 football team">Spain's under-19</a>, for whom he played six international matches. During the <a href="/wiki/2004_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2004 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2004 U19 Euro</a>, Ramos was a key figure for Spain as he started in four out of five of their matches on the way to winning their second U19 European Championship, including scoring a decisive penalty in the Semi-final penalty-shoot out against <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_under-19_football_team" title="Ukraine national under-19 football team">Ukraine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> On 26 March 2005, in a 3–0 <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game" title="Exhibition game">friendly</a> win over <a href="/wiki/China_PR_national_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="China PR national football team">China</a> in <a href="/wiki/Salamanca" title="Salamanca">Salamanca</a>, he first appeared for the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">senior side</a> at only 18 years and 361 days of age, making him the youngest player to play for the national team in the last 55 years. He held this record until 1 March 2006, when it was broken by <a href="/wiki/Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas" title="Cesc Fàbregas">Cesc Fàbregas</a> in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast_national_football_team" title="Ivory Coast national football team">Côte d'Ivoire</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 October 2005, Ramos scored his first two international goals in a 6–0 away thrashing of <a href="/wiki/San_Marino_national_football_team" title="San Marino national football team">San Marino</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006 FIFA World Cup</a> <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2006 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">qualifiers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> He was selected for the final stages in Germany and, after the international retirement of Real Madrid teammate <a href="/wiki/M%C3%ADchel_Salgado" title="Míchel Salgado">Míchel Salgado</a>, became the undisputed first-choice right-back. Despite wearing the number 4 jersey for Real Madrid, Ramos admitted he wears the number 15 for Spain in memory of his close friend and former Sevilla teammate Puerta, who died in August 2007 and made his Spain debut wearing No. 15.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2008">Euro 2008</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ramos_Euro_2012_vs_France_02.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Sergio_Ramos_Euro_2012_vs_France_02.jpg/240px-Sergio_Ramos_Euro_2012_vs_France_02.jpg" decoding="async" width="240" height="160" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Sergio_Ramos_Euro_2012_vs_France_02.jpg/360px-Sergio_Ramos_Euro_2012_vs_France_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Sergio_Ramos_Euro_2012_vs_France_02.jpg/480px-Sergio_Ramos_Euro_2012_vs_France_02.jpg 2x" data-file-width="656" data-file-height="436" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Ramos_Euro_2012_vs_France_02.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ramos at the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">Euro 2012</a>, in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_knockout_phase#Spain_vs_France" title="UEFA Euro 2012 knockout phase">quarter-final match against France</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Throughout Spain's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">UEFA Euro 2008</a> <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2008 qualifying">qualifying campaign</a>, Ramos was a regular member of the starting eleven as the national side finished first in its group, above <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a>. He scored two goals, including one in a 3–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/Denmark_national_football_team" title="Denmark national football team">Denmark</a>, in 11 appearances. In the tournament's final stages, Ramos played in all matches and minutes, except the 2–1 group stage win against <a href="/wiki/Greece_national_football_team" title="Greece national football team">Greece</a>. In <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2008 Final">the final</a>, his pass nearly set up <a href="/wiki/Marcos_Senna" title="Marcos Senna">Marcos Senna</a>'s first international goal, but the latter missed his opportunity by inches. During the celebrations after the 1–0 defeat of <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a>, he wore a T-shirt in honour of his late friend Puerta.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2009_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_and_2010_FIFA_World_Cup">2009 FIFA Confederations Cup and 2010 FIFA World Cup</span></h3>
<p>Ramos was selected in the squad for the <a href="/wiki/2009_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2009 FIFA Confederations Cup">2009 FIFA Confederations Cup</a> in South Africa, as Spain finished in third.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup>
On 3 June 2010, he captained Spain for the first time, in a 1–0 friendly win over <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_football_team" title="South Korea national football team">South Korea</a> in <a href="/wiki/Innsbruck" title="Innsbruck">Innsbruck</a>, Austria.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 World Cup</a>, held in the same country, Ramos played every minute of the tournament as a right back, helping Spain keep five <a href="/wiki/Shutout" title="Shutout">clean sheets</a> and reach <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2010 FIFA World Cup Final">the final</a>, which they won 1–0 against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a>; he topped the tournament's <a href="/wiki/Castrol_Performance_Index" class="mw-redirect" title="Castrol Performance Index">Castrol Performance Index</a> with a score of 9.79.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> Despite playing at right-back, he also completed more <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">solo runs</a> than any other player in the tournament, 31.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2012">Euro 2012</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:233px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Torres,_Mata_and_Ramos_Euro_2012_trophy_01.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Torres%2C_Mata_and_Ramos_Euro_2012_trophy_01.jpg/231px-Torres%2C_Mata_and_Ramos_Euro_2012_trophy_01.jpg" decoding="async" width="231" height="176" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Torres%2C_Mata_and_Ramos_Euro_2012_trophy_01.jpg/347px-Torres%2C_Mata_and_Ramos_Euro_2012_trophy_01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Torres%2C_Mata_and_Ramos_Euro_2012_trophy_01.jpg/462px-Torres%2C_Mata_and_Ramos_Euro_2012_trophy_01.jpg 2x" data-file-width="656" data-file-height="499" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Torres,_Mata_and_Ramos_Euro_2012_trophy_01.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Fernando_Torres" title="Fernando Torres">Fernando Torres</a> (l), <a href="/wiki/Juan_Mata" title="Juan Mata">Juan Mata</a> and Ramos holding the <a href="/wiki/Henri_Delaunay_Trophy" class="mw-redirect" title="Henri Delaunay Trophy">Henri Delaunay Trophy</a> after winning the 14th <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship" title="UEFA European Championship">European Championship</a></div></div></div>
<p>Ramos returned to the heart of the defence for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">Euro 2012</a>. When asked about his role change, he replied: "I have adapted and feel comfortable in the middle, but I am a World and European champion at right-back".<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> He played all the games in <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> alongside Barcelona's <a href="/wiki/Gerard_Piqu%C3%A9" title="Gerard Piqué">Gerard Piqué</a> and, in the semi-finals against <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a>, he converted his penalty shootout attempt in an eventual 4–2 win (0–0 after 120 minutes), scoring for the eventual champions in <a href="/wiki/Anton%C3%ADn_Panenka" title="Antonín Panenka">Panenka</a>-style.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> On 1 July, Ramos won his third trophy with the Spanish senior National Team as they thrashed Italy 4–0 in the Final. Ramos' performances during the Euro earned him a place in the Team of The Tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> Ramos wore another T-shirt during Spain's Euro 2012 celebrations to pay homage to his late friend Puerta.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_and_2014_FIFA_World_Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup and 2014 FIFA World Cup</span></h3>
<p>On 22 March 2013, Ramos celebrated his 100th <a href="/wiki/Cap_(sport)" title="Cap (sport)">cap</a> by opening the scoring in a 1–1 draw with <a href="/wiki/Finland_national_football_team" title="Finland national football team">Finland</a> in <a href="/wiki/Gij%C3%B3n" title="Gijón">Gijón</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">2014 World Cup qualifiers</a>. He became the youngest European player ever to reach that figure in the process, surpassing Germany's <a href="/wiki/Lukas_Podolski" title="Lukas Podolski">Lukas Podolski</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Young_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Young-8">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> In June, Ramos contested in the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</a> in Brazil, starting every match as Spain lost to the hosts in <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_Final" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup Final">the final</a>. He captained the side for their second <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_Final" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup Final">group</a> game, a 10–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Tahiti_national_football_team" title="Tahiti national football team">Tahiti</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Maracan%C3%A3_Stadium" title="Maracanã Stadium">Maracanã</a>, which is the biggest win of his career.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> On 30 June, he missed a penalty kick in the 3–0 <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_Final" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup Final">Confederations Cup Final</a> loss to <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ramos was selected for his third <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> He played the full 90 minutes of each of the team's matches in Brazil, each with a different partner in central defence, as the reigning champions were eliminated from the group stage.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2016_and_2018_FIFA_World_Cup">Euro 2016 and 2018 FIFA World Cup</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Russia-Spain_2017_(1).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Russia-Spain_2017_%281%29.jpg/230px-Russia-Spain_2017_%281%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="230" height="174" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Russia-Spain_2017_%281%29.jpg/345px-Russia-Spain_2017_%281%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4f/Russia-Spain_2017_%281%29.jpg/460px-Russia-Spain_2017_%281%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1235" data-file-height="936" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Russia-Spain_2017_(1).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ramos celebrates after scoring a goal against <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a> in a friendly in <a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a>.</div></div></div>
