<p>In February 2016, Ramos won the <a href="/wiki/Luis_Aragon%C3%A9s" title="Luis Aragonés">Luis Aragonés</a> Award by <a href="/wiki/Marca_(newspaper)" title="Marca (newspaper)">Marca</a> which distinguished him as the best player of the national team in the past year.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> With <a href="/wiki/David_de_Gea" title="David de Gea">David de Gea</a> selected ahead of Iker Casillas in Spain's starting line-up, Ramos captained the team at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>. On 21 June 2016, he had a penalty kick saved by <a href="/wiki/Danijel_Suba%C5%A1i%C4%87" title="Danijel Subaši">Danijel Subaši</a> in a 2–1 loss to <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> Spain finished their Euro group as runners-up and crashed out in the Round of 16 against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 23 March 2018, days before turning 32, Ramos earned his 150th cap for Spain in a 1–1 friendly draw with Germany in <a href="/wiki/D%C3%BCsseldorf" title="Düsseldorf">Düsseldorf</a>. Only <a href="/wiki/Iker_Casillas" title="Iker Casillas">Iker Casillas</a> had previously reached the mark for the team.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ramos was included in the Spain <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_squads" title="2018 FIFA World Cup squads">squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> and would go into his fourth tournament, and first World Cup as Captain after Iker Casillas missed out.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> He played in all three of Spain's Group stage matches as they topped the 'Group of Death' ahead of European Champions Portugal.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup#Round_of_16" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">Round of 16</a> against <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a>, Ramos believed he scored the opening goal but it was later credited as an <a href="/wiki/Sergei_Ignashevich" title="Sergei Ignashevich">Sergei Ignashevich</a> own goal.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> The match ended 1–1 after Extra Time and was decided on penalties (4–2) as the hosts eliminated La Roja. Ramos scored Spain's fourth penalty but it wasn't enough as teammates <a href="/wiki/Koke_(footballer,_born_1992)" title="Koke (footballer, born 1992)">Koke</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iago_Aspas" title="Iago Aspas">Aspas</a> both had their penalties saved.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:ESP-RUS_(2).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/ESP-RUS_%282%29.jpg/220px-ESP-RUS_%282%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="135" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/ESP-RUS_%282%29.jpg/330px-ESP-RUS_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/ESP-RUS_%282%29.jpg/440px-ESP-RUS_%282%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="918" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:ESP-RUS_(2).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ramos with <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a> Captain <a href="/wiki/Igor_Akinfeev" title="Igor Akinfeev">Igor Akinfeev</a> (r) and referee <a href="/wiki/Bj%C3%B6rn_Kuipers" title="Björn Kuipers">Björn Kuipers</a> before the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> Round of 16 match at the <a href="/wiki/Luzhniki_Stadium" title="Luzhniki Stadium">Luzhniki Stadium</a> in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a>.</div></div></div>
<h3><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_UEFA_Nations_League_and_Euro_2020_qualification"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_UEFA_Nations_League_and_Euro_2020_qualification">2018–19 UEFA Nations League and Euro 2020 qualification</span></h3>
<p>With new coach <a href="/wiki/Luis_Enrique_(footballer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Luis Enrique (footballer)">Luis Enrique</a>, Ramos retained captaincy of the national team. He played in all four of Spain's <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Nations_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Nations League">2018–19 UEFA Nations League</a> group matches, becoming the nation's top scorer in the group with three goals – scoring once against England and twice against Croatia.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> Spain finished second in their UEFA Nations League Group, which saw them miss out on the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Nations_League_Finals" title="2019 UEFA Nations League Finals">2019 UEFA Nations League Finals</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> In March 2019, Ramos scored the winner in Spain's first <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2020 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2020 qualifying</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Norway_national_football_team" title="Norway national football team">Norway</a> through another <a href="/wiki/Panenka_(penalty_kick)" title="Panenka (penalty kick)">Panenka</a> penalty in a 2–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> This was his tenth penalty of the season, scoring them all. It was also his fifth consecutive match scoring for Spain, which is a personal record.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> Spain manager Enrique hailed Ramos as a 'unique player in history' after the match.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the second Euro 2020 qualification match, away to <a href="/wiki/Malta_national_football_team" title="Malta national football team">Malta</a>, Ramos did not score for the first time in six matches for Spain – failing to extend his scoring streak. However, the match ended 2–0 to Spain which was his 121st win with La Roja, equaling the all-time record of Iker Casillas.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> On 7 June 2019, Ramos broke the record of most international victories with 122, following a 4–1 victory against the <a href="/wiki/Faroe_Islands_national_football_team" title="Faroe Islands national football team">Faroe Islands</a>, scoring Spain's opening goal in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, ahead of the match against Sweden, Ramos received a plaque from the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Football_Federation" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish Football Federation">Spanish Football Federation</a> to commemorate his record.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> The match ended with a 3–0 win for Spain, where he scored the first goal and extended his tally to 123 international victories.<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup> On 5 September 2019, Ramos scored from a penalty kick his 21st international goal to open the score in Spain's 2–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a> in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2020 qualifying">Euro 2020 qualifier</a>, which made him the joint 10th top scorer in the history of the national team, alonsigde <a href="/wiki/M%C3%ADchel_(footballer,_born_1963)" title="Míchel (footballer, born 1963)">Míchel</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> On 8 September, Ramos won his 167th cap for Spain in a 4–0 home win over the Faroe Islands in a Euro 2020 qualifier; with this appearance, he equaled Iker Casillas as Spain's most capped player of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> On 12 October 2019, he became the nation's sole <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team#Most_capped_players" title="Spain national football team">most capped</a> player.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_UEFA_Nations_League"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_UEFA_Nations_League">2020–21 UEFA Nations League</span></h3>
<p>On 6 September 2020, Ramos scored a brace in a 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_football_team" title="Ukraine national football team">Ukraine</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Nations_League_A#Group_4" title="2020–21 UEFA Nations League A">2020–21 UEFA Nations League</a>, reaching 23 international goals and equaling <a href="/wiki/Alfredo_Di_St%C3%A9fano" title="Alfredo Di Stéfano">Alfredo Di Stéfano</a> as Spain's eighth-highest all-time goalscorer.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup> On 14 November 2020, in a 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a>, he made his 177th appearance for Spain and overtook <a href="/wiki/Gianluigi_Buffon" title="Gianluigi Buffon">Gianluigi Buffon</a>'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_men%27s_footballers_with_100_or_more_international_caps" title="List of men&#39;s footballers with 100 or more international caps">record for the most international caps received by a European player</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Player_profile">Player profile</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span></h3>
<p>Regarded as one of the best defenders in the world, and of his generation, Ramos is a physically strong player who excels in the air due to his elevation, eye for goal, and heading accuracy, making him a goal threat on set-pieces;<sup id="cite_ref-best_player_186-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_player-186">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_defenders_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_defenders-6">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-calciomercato.it_187-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-calciomercato.it-187">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-A_closer_look_at_Spain’s_Euro_2012_squad_190-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_closer_look_at_Spain’s_Euro_2012_squad-190">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> he is also a competent and aggressive tackler. In addition to his defensive skills and goalscoring ability,<sup id="cite_ref-best_player_186-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_player-186">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_defenders_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_defenders-6">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> he is gifted with pace,<sup id="cite_ref-calciomercato.it_187-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-calciomercato.it-187">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> and is comfortable on the ball,<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup> possessing good technical ability, as well as good distribution, passing, and <a href="/wiki/Cross_(association_football)" title="Cross (association football)">crossing</a> ability,<sup id="cite_ref-best_player_186-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_player-186">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio_Ramos_the_best_defender_in_the_world-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_defenders_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_defenders-6">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Ancelotti:_Ramos_like_Maldini_193-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ancelotti:_Ramos_like_Maldini-193">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> which allows him to carry the ball forward,<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> switch the play with long balls, or play out from the back on the ground.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> According to Spanish sports newspaper <a href="/wiki/Marca_(newspaper)" title="Marca (newspaper)"><i>Marca</i></a>, <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a>'s official records confirmed that in 2015, Ramos was clocked at a sprinting speed of 30.6 kilometers per hour, making him one of the fastest footballers in the world at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup> He is also an accurate <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a> taker, and is known for often using the Panenka technique when taking them.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> He has also been known to take <a href="/wiki/Free_kick_(association_football)" title="Free kick (association football)">free kicks</a>, courtesy of his ability to <a href="/wiki/Curl_(association_football)" title="Curl (association football)">bend</a> the ball and his powerful striking ability from distance.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ramos has earned plaudits for his leadership, athleticism, technical prowess, and his ability to excel both offensively and defensively, as well as his versatility, which allows him to be deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre-back" title="Defender (association football)">centre back</a> and as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">full back</a>; in his youth, he often played as a right-back, while he later established himself as a centre-back as his career progressed. Due to his wide range of skills, his former Real Madrid manager <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ancelotti" title="Carlo Ancelotti">Carlo Ancelotti</a> has compared him to legendary defender <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Maldini" title="Paolo Maldini">Paolo Maldini</a>; he went on to describe him as "the best defender in the world at the moment" in 2014,<sup id="cite_ref-A_closer_look_at_Spain’s_Euro_2012_squad_190-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_closer_look_at_Spain’s_Euro_2012_squad-190">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Ancelotti:_Ramos_like_Maldini_193-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ancelotti:_Ramos_like_Maldini-193">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup> a view which was echoed by <a href="/wiki/Giorgio_Chiellini" title="Giorgio Chiellini">Giorgio Chiellini</a> in 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-Masterstroke_206-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Masterstroke-206">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup> Ramos has also occasionally been deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central</a> or <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>, in particular under Ancelotti during the 2014–15 season.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup> Ramos has been praised for his decisive performances in important games, most notably for Real Madrid, due to his tendency to score crucial goals for his team, and is considered by several pundits to be one of the most reliable performers in high-pressure situations.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;B&#93;</a></sup> However, despite his ability as a defender, his tactical sense, consistency, and concentration from match to match have been questioned at times by pundits and other footballing figures, who have accused him of being too impulsive in his challenges or prone to occasional defensive errors throughout the course a season.<sup id="cite_ref-A_closer_look_at_Spain’s_Euro_2012_squad_190-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_closer_look_at_Spain’s_Euro_2012_squad-190">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Masterstroke_206-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Masterstroke-206">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ramos is also often criticised in the media for using excessive, reckless force while playing, as well as for his lack of discipline and tendency to pick-up an excessive number of unnecessary cards;<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup> he has also been accused of <a href="/wiki/Diving_(association_football)" title="Diving (association football)">diving</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Disciplinary_record">Disciplinary record</span></h3>
<p>Ramos holds multiple disciplinary records, for Real Madrid, in the Champions League, La Liga, <i>El Clásico</i>, and in the Spanish national team.<sup id="cite_ref-beast_222-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-beast-222">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ramos holds the record for most carded player in La Liga, with 191 cards. His 171 yellow cards surpass <a href="/wiki/Alberto_Lopo" title="Alberto Lopo">Alberto Lopo</a>, the former record holder for La Liga yellow cards.<sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup> The remaining 20 are red cards, making Ramos the most sent-off player in La Liga as well. His La Liga card record is higher than any other player's in the major European leagues, making him the most booked player in all major European top divisions.<sup id="cite_ref-records_224-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-records-224">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the Champions League, Ramos has amassed 40 yellow cards and 4 red cards (3 of which were straight red cards), making him both the most-carded player and joint-most red-carded player in Champions League history.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Lastly, Ramos also holds the record for being the most carded player in the history of the Spanish national team, with 24 yellow cards.<sup id="cite_ref-records_224-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-records-224">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>
<p>Ramos entered a relationship with journalist/presenter <a href="/wiki/Pilar_Rubio" title="Pilar Rubio">Pilar Rubio</a> in September 2012. This was confirmed by both at the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Ballon_d%27Or" title="FIFA Ballon d&#39;Or">FIFA Ballon d'Or</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup> They have four sons together: Sergio Jr (born 6 May 2014), Marco (born 27 November 2015), Alejandro (born 25 March 2018) and Maximo Adriano (born 26 July 2020).<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup> On 16 July 2018, Ramos proposed to Pilar Rubio and the couple got engaged.<sup id="cite_ref-231" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-231">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup> The couple married in Ramos' home-town of Seville on 15 June 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ramos has been described as a 'family person' and has a close relationship with his siblings and parents.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup> Rene, Ramos' brother, is currently his <a href="/wiki/Football_agent" class="mw-redirect" title="Football agent">football agent</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup> Ramos is a fan of <a href="/wiki/Bullfighting" title="Bullfighting">bullfighting</a> and he is a personal friend of matador Alejandro Talavante.<sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup> He celebrated victories for both club and country by playing with a matador's cape.<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup> Ramos is also a keen horse aficionado, owning a <a href="/wiki/Stud_farm" title="Stud farm">stud farm</a> in his native <a href="/wiki/Andalusia" title="Andalusia">Andalusia</a> specifically dedicated to the breeding of the <a href="/wiki/Andalusian_horse" title="Andalusian horse">Andalusian horse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup> Ramos' horse, 'Yucatán SR4' became a World Champion in 2018.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Body_art">Body art</span></h3>
<p>Ramos is <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church_in_Spain" title="Catholic Church in Spain">Catholic</a>, and has a tattoo of <a href="/wiki/Mary,_mother_of_Jesus" title="Mary, mother of Jesus">Mary</a> which covers the top half of his left arm.<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup> However, he has more than 42 tattoos, including <a href="/wiki/Star_of_David" title="Star of David">Star of David</a> in honor of his grandmother, Nena, who gave a pendant of the same design to his mother; in addition, he also has tattoos of a lion, wolf, <a href="/wiki/Dreamcatcher" title="Dreamcatcher">dreamcatcher</a>, map of Spain, <a href="/wiki/Native_Americans_in_the_United_States" title="Native Americans in the United States">Native American</a> chief, <a href="/wiki/Jesus" title="Jesus">Jesus Christ</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hamsa" title="Hamsa">Hamsa</a>, FIFA World Cup and Champions League trophies, his family members, and lots of others.<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Amazon_Prime_documentary">Amazon Prime documentary</span></h3>
<p>In January 2019, <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Prime" title="Amazon Prime">Amazon Prime</a> and Ramos himself announced they will release an eight-episode documentary series on Ramos' life on and off the pitch known as <i>El Corazón de Sergio Ramos</i> (<i>The Heart of Sergio Ramos</i>). This would be the first ever time the public would see the personal side of Ramos and his family.<sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup> On 5 March, during Real Madrid's <a href="/wiki/Champions_League_2018-19" class="mw-redirect" title="Champions League 2018-19">Champions League Round of 16</a> second leg match, Ramos was suspended and watched the match from his VIP area in the stands. His reactions were filmed by the Amazon Prime crew.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;239&#93;</a></sup> This sparked controversy as Real Madrid lost the match and were eliminated from the Champions League, though Ramos suggested on his social media networks that there were "certain commitments made and it never remotely went through my head that the game could have turned out as it did".<sup id="cite_ref-marca.com_100-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-marca.com-100">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to the success of his first docu-series with Amazon, Ramos announced in June 2020 via his social media accounts that Amazon Prime will be releasing another documentary known as <i>La Leyenda Sergio Ramos</i> (<i>The Legend of Sergio Ramos</i>), which highlights his career's most defining moments. It is expected to be released in 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242">&#91;240&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
